# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Java Dependency Injection with Kafka Plugin Architecture

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the plugin/extension loading system: the PluginClassLoader, the plugin scanning via reflection, and the interface-based dependency injection used for Connector, Converter, and HeaderConverter plugins.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Perfect! I've successfully created the `answer.json` file with a comprehensive analysis of Apache Kafka's Java plugin/extension loading system. 

## Summary

The answer includes **21 Java source files** that implement Kafka's sophisticated plugin architecture:

### Core Components Found:

1. **ClassLoader Isolation** (3 files):
   - `PluginClassLoader` - Custom URLClassLoader for isolated plugin loading
   - `DelegatingClassLoader` - Routes class loading to appropriate plugin classloaders
   - `ClassLoaderFactory` - Factory for creating classloaders

2. **Plugin Discovery via Reflection** (4 files):
   - `PluginScanner` - Abstract base for plugin scanning
   - `ReflectionScanner` - Reflection-based discovery using Classgraph
   - `ServiceLoaderScanner` - Java ServiceLoader-based discovery
   - `PluginSource` - Represents plugin source locations

3. **Plugin Metadata** (4 files):
   - `PluginDesc<T>` - Generic descriptor for discovered plugins
   - `PluginType` - Enum of plugin interface types
   - `PluginScanResult` - Container for scan results

4. **Interface-Based Plugin Types** (5 files):
   - `Converter` - For serialization/deserialization
   - `HeaderConverter` - For header processing
   - `SinkConnector` - Write connectors
   - `SourceConnector` - Read connectors
   - `Connector` - Base connector interface

5. **Dependency Injection** (2 files):
   - `Plugins` - Central DI container and service locator
   - `LoaderSwap` - Context classloader swapping utility

The system enables flexible, extensible plugin architecture through ClassLoader isolation combined with reflection-based and ServiceLoader-based discovery, allowing plugins with different dependencies to coexist safely.

classloading. The system is located in the 'sg-evals/kafka--0753c489' repository under the connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ package.\\n\\n## Core Architecture\\n\\n### ClassLoader Hierarchy\\nThe system uses a custom classloader hierarchy to provide plugin isolation:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that extends URLClassLoader and implements child-first delegation for loading isolated plugins. Each plugin location gets its own PluginClassLoader instance.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A URLClassLoader that delegates class loading to multiple PluginClassLoader instances based on the requested class. It maintains a registry of discovered plugins and routes class loading requests to the appropriate PluginClassLoader.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory class that creates both DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances with support for security manager compatibility.\\n\\n### Plugin Discovery Mechanism\\n\\nThe plugin scanning system uses reflection and Java ServiceLoader to discover plugins:\\n\\n1. **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java): Abstract base class defining the plugin scanning interface with methods to discover plugins from plugin sources.\\n\\n2. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Classgraph library to perform reflection-based discovery. It scans for concrete implementations of plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy) and collects version information via plugin reflection.\\n\\n3. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Java's ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins registered in META-INF/services/ configuration files.\\n\\n4. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A Java record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, multi-JAR directory, or class hierarchy), including the ClassLoader and URLs to scan.\\n\\n### Plugin Metadata and Description\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc<T>** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): Generic descriptor class that holds metadata for a discovered plugin including the plugin class, version, type, and associated ClassLoader. Implements Comparable for sorting plugins by version and location.\\n\\n2. **PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java): Enumeration of plugin interface types: SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_POLICY.\\n\\n3. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Container for scan results holding sorted sets of PluginDesc instances for each plugin type, with support for merging multiple scan results.\\n\\n### Interface-Based Plugin Types\\n\\nThe system supports the following plugin interfaces:\\n\\n1. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for translating between Kafka Connect's runtime data format and byte[]. Supports ServiceLoader discovery and metrics registration.\\n\\n2. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Similar to Converter but specifically for processing message headers.\\n\\n3. **SinkConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that write data from Kafka to external systems.\\n\\n4. **SourceConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that read data from external systems into Kafka.\\n\\n5. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base abstract class for both source and sink connectors defining the common interface.\\n\\n### Dependency Injection via Plugins Class\\n\\nThe **Plugins** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) serves as the central dependency injection container that:\\n\\n1. **Initialization**: Constructor accepts configuration properties, discovers plugin locations, creates DelegatingClassLoader, and scans for plugins using both ReflectionScanner and ServiceLoaderScanner based on PluginDiscoveryMode.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Discovery Flow**: initLoaders() method orchestrates the scanning process:\\n   - Calls ServiceLoaderScanner.discoverPlugins() for SERVICE_LOAD mode\\n   - Calls ReflectionScanner.discoverPlugins() for ONLY_SCAN mode\\n   - Merges results and installs them in DelegatingClassLoader\\n   - Reports compatibility issues if plugins lack ServiceLoader manifests\\n\\n3. **Plugin Instantiation**: Provides methods like newConverter(), newHeaderConverter(), newConnector() that:\\n   - Load the plugin class using the appropriate ClassLoader\\n   - Swap the thread context ClassLoader to the plugin's ClassLoader\\n   - Instantiate the plugin using Utils.newInstance()\\n   - Configure the plugin if it implements Configurable\\n\\n4. **ClassLoader Swapping**: Uses LoaderSwap (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java) to safely swap the thread context ClassLoader during plugin instantiation and initialization.\\n\\n5. **Plugin Querying**: Provides accessor methods for different plugin types (converters(), headerConverters(), sinkConnectors(), sourceConnectors(), etc.) that query PluginScanResult.\\n\\n### Utility Functions\\n\\n**PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) provides utility methods for:\\n- Determining plugin locations from configuration\\n- Creating plugin sources (classpath and isolated)\\n- Checking if classes should be loaded in isolation\\n- Computing plugin aliases for shorthand reference\\n- Managing plugin version requirements\\n\\n### Configuration and Recommendations\\n\\n**PluginsRecommenders** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java) provides ConfigDef Recommender implementations for plugin configuration fields, enabling dynamic discovery and recommendation of available plugins.\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe plugin system uses ClassLoader isolation combined with reflection-based and ServiceLoader-based discovery to provide flexible, extensible plugin architecture. The Plugins class acts as a service locator/dependency injector, managing plugin lifecycle including discovery, instantiation, and dependency injection through a type-safe interface-based architecture. The LoaderSwap pattern ensures proper ClassLoader management throughout the plugin lifecycle, enabling plugins with different dependencies to coexist without conflicts.\"\n}\n",

Each plugin location gets its own PluginClassLoader instance.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A URLClassLoader that delegates class loading to multiple PluginClassLoader instances based on the requested class. It maintains a registry of discovered plugins and routes class loading requests to the appropriate PluginClassLoader.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java): Factory class that creates both DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances with support for security manager compatibility.\\n\\n### Plugin Discovery Mechanism\\n\\nThe plugin scanning system uses reflection and Java ServiceLoader to discover plugins:\\n\\n1. **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java): Abstract base class defining the plugin scanning interface with methods to discover plugins from plugin sources.\\n\\n2. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Classgraph library to perform reflection-based discovery. It scans for concrete implementations of plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy) and collects version information via plugin reflection.\\n\\n3. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Implements scanPlugins() using Java's ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins registered in META-INF/services/ configuration files.\\n\\n4. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A Java record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, multi-JAR directory, or class hierarchy), including the ClassLoader and URLs to scan.\\n\\n### Plugin Metadata and Description\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc<T>** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): Generic descriptor class that holds metadata for a discovered plugin including the plugin class, version, type, and associated ClassLoader. Implements Comparable for sorting plugins by version and location.\\n\\n2. **PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java): Enumeration of plugin interface types: SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_POLICY.\\n\\n3. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Container for scan results holding sorted sets of PluginDesc instances for each plugin type, with support for merging multiple scan results.\\n\\n### Interface-Based Plugin Types\\n\\nThe system supports the following plugin interfaces:\\n\\n1. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for translating between Kafka Connect's runtime data format and byte[]. Supports ServiceLoader discovery and metrics registration.\\n\\n2. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Similar to Converter but specifically for processing message headers.\\n\\n3. **SinkConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that write data from Kafka to external systems.\\n\\n4. **SourceConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java): Abstract class for connectors that read data from external systems into Kafka.\\n\\n5. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base abstract class for both source and sink connectors defining the common interface.\\n\\n### Dependency Injection via Plugins Class\\n\\nThe **Plugins** class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) serves as the central dependency injection container that:\\n\\n1. **Initialization**: Constructor accepts configuration properties, discovers plugin locations, creates DelegatingClassLoader, and scans for plugins using both ReflectionScanner and ServiceLoaderScanner based on PluginDiscoveryMode.\\n\\n2. **Plugin Discovery Flow**: initLoaders() method orchestrates the scanning process:\\n   - Calls ServiceLoaderScanner.discoverPlugins() for SERVICE_LOAD mode\\n   - Calls ReflectionScanner.discoverPlugins() for ONLY_SCAN mode\\n   - Merges results and installs them in DelegatingClassLoader\\n   - Reports compatibility issues if plugins lack ServiceLoader manifests\\n\\n3. **Plugin Instantiation**: Provides methods like newConverter(), newHeaderConverter(), newConnector() that:\\n   - Load the plugin class using the appropriate ClassLoader\\n   - Swap the thread context ClassLoader to the plugin's ClassLoader\\n   - Instantiate the plugin using Utils.newInstance()\\n   - Configure the plugin if it implements Configurable\\n\\n4. **ClassLoader Swapping**: Uses LoaderSwap (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java) to safely swap the thread context ClassLoader during plugin instantiation and initialization.\\n\\n5. **Plugin Querying**: Provides accessor methods for different plugin types (converters(), headerConverters(), sinkConnectors(), sourceConnectors(), etc.) that query PluginScanResult.\\n\\n### Utility Functions\\n\\n**PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) provides utility methods for:\\n- Determining plugin locations from configuration\\n- Creating plugin sources (classpath and isolated)\\n- Checking if classes should be loaded in isolation\\n- Computing plugin aliases for shorthand reference\\n- Managing plugin version requirements\\n\\n### Configuration and Recommendations\\n\\n**PluginsRecommenders** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java) provides ConfigDef Recommender implementations for plugin configuration fields, enabling dynamic discovery and recommendation of available plugins.\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe plugin system uses ClassLoader isolation combined with reflection-based and ServiceLoader-based discovery to provide flexible, extensible plugin architecture. The Plugins class acts as a service locator/dependency injector, managing plugin lifecycle including discovery, instantiation, and dependency injection through a type-safe interface-based architecture. The LoaderSwap pattern ensures proper ClassLoader management throughout the plugin lifecycle, enabling plugins with different dependencies to coexist without conflicts.\"\n}\n",
